# Deployment Summary: 2025-11-11

- **Commit:** `c59658a`
- **Timestamp:** `2025-11-11 19:22:49`

## Commit Message

```
feat: Implement persistent cart state and UI improvements

- Add CartContext for global state management with localStorage persistence
- Implement persistent cart state across all pages and browser sessions
- Add persistent tree expansion and search query state
- Add persistent currently viewed KPI in detail preview
- Fix metadata service loader to recursively load KPIs from subdirectories (SCOR KPIs now load)
- Add 'View Full Details' button to KPI preview panel
- Implement functional 'Add to Cart' button on KPI Detail Page
- Update ConfigPage to use cart context instead of local state
- Update MetricTree to use cart context for expansion and search
- Update KPIDetailPage with cart integration and status display
- Fix split-panel preview behavior (clicking KPI shows preview, not full page)
- Add comprehensive KPI Detail Page with 5 tabs and full metadata
- Add Object Model Viewer page with UML diagrams
- Document all changes in CHANGELOG.md

Storage keys:
- analytics_kpi_cart: Cart items
- analytics_current_view_kpi: Currently viewed KPI
- analytics_tree_expanded: Expanded tree nodes
- analytics_tree_search: Search query
```
